The concept of \"Power of 3\" signifies that market makers' algorithms perform three essential actions related to price on each trading day.\n\nThese three actions are categorized as Accumulation, Manipulation, and Distribution, often abbreviated as AMD:\n\nAccumulation: In this phase, market makers gather liquidity by creating a ranging market. The purpose of establishing a ranging market is to entice both buyers and sellers to enter the market, believing that the price will move in their favor.\n\nManipulation: Following the accumulation of both buying and selling orders, market makers manipulate the market to attract another group of traders known as breakout traders. However, this manipulation is not their intended direction for the day. It is merely a tactic to increase liquidity. This increased liquidity then guides them to their next step, which is moving and distributing the price according to their actual plan for the day.\n\nDistribution: After manipulating the price in a specific direction different from their initial plan, market makers then distribute the price in their originally intended direction. For instance, if their intention is to buy, they will initially sell in the market and subsequently purchase at a discounted price level.\n\n*Pictures 1: The Theory of ICT Po3\n\n*Pictures 2: Examples of the application of ICT Po3 on the BTC/USDT price chart \n\nLet's look forward to \"PART II: Applications of ICT Power of 3.\"\n\n#Bitcoin #USDT #Crypto #cryptocurrency #Po3 #ICTPo3 #midnightclub #Powerof3", "replyCount": 61, "retweetCount": 0, "likeCount": 55, "quoteCount": 0, "conversationId": 1710606173324656902, "hashtags": [], "cashtags": [], "mentionedUsers": [], "links": [], "viewCount": 438, "retweetedTweet": null, "quotedTweet": null, "place": null, "coordinates": null, "inReplyToTweetId": null, "inReplyToUser": null, "source": "<a href=\"https://mobile.twitter.com\" rel=\"nofollow\">Twitter Web App</a>", "sourceUrl": "https://mobile.twitter.com", "sourceLabel": "Twitter Web App", "media": {"photos": [{"url": "https://pbs.twimg.com/media/F71J9oNaIAAK7IX.png"}, {"url": "https://pbs.twimg.com/media/F71J_B_aYAAk6DI.png"}], "videos": [], "animated": []}, "_type": "snscrape.modules.twitter.Tweet"}

C\u00f4ng ty m\u00ecnh \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c c\u00e1i c\u0169ng nhi\u1ec1u th\u00e0nh ph\u1ea7n \u1ed1ng kh\u00f3i n\u00ean m\u1ed7i l\u1ea7n ra ban c\u00f4ng th\u01b0\u1eddng l\u00e0 m\u00ecnh c\u00f3 b\u1ea1n, chia nhau t\u00ed l\u1eeda, n\u00f3i d\u0103m ba c\u00e2u chuy\u1ec7n phi\u1ebfm. T\u1eeb ng\u00e0y d\u1eebng h\u00fat thu\u1ed1c, m\u00ecnh c\u0169ng tr\u00e1nh lu\u00f4n c\u00e1i khu v\u1ef1c \u1ea5y, ho\u1eb7c c\u0169ng l\u1ef1a l\u00fac n\u00e0o v\u1eafng ng\u01b0\u1eddi m\u1edbi ra \u0111\u1ee9ng m\u1ed9t ch\u00fat.\n\nH\u00f4m nay khi m\u00ecnh b\u01b0\u1edbc ra ban c\u00f4ng tr\u01b0\u1edbc gi\u1edd l\u00e0m \u0111\u1ec3 g\u1ecdi \u0111i\u1ec7n v\u1ec1 cho con , m\u1eb7c d\u00f9 \u0111\u1ebfn s\u1edbm kh\u00f4ng c\u00f3 ai , nh\u01b0ng tr\u00ean b\u00e0n c\u00f3 bao thu\u1ed1c . \n\nNh\u00ecn bao thu\u1ed1c l\u00e1 tr\u00ean b\u00e0n, m\u00ecnh c\u0169ng c\u00f3 nh\u1eefng c\u1ea3m x\u00fac kh\u00f3 t\u1ea3. Kh\u00f4ng kh\u00f3 \u0111\u1ec3 nh\u1eadn ra hi\u1ec7n t\u01b0\u1ee3ng x\u00e3 h\u1ed9i c\u0169ng gi\u1ed1ng v\u1edbi th\u1eddi trang \u1edf vi\u1ec7c n\u00f3 lu\u00f4n quay v\u00f2ng, v\u00e0 s\u1ef1 nguy hi\u1ec3m c\u1ee7a ch\u1ee7 ngh\u0129a ti\u00eau th\u1ee5 trong b\u1ed1i c\u1ea3nh kinh t\u1ebf bi\u1ebfn \u0111\u1ed9ng v\u00e0 nh\u1eefng cu\u1ed9c kh\u1ee7ng ho\u1ea3ng kinh t\u1ebf c\u00e1ch \u0111\u00e2y m\u1ed9t th\u1eadp k\u1ef7 l\u00e0 y\u1ebfu t\u1ed1 c\u0103n b\u1ea3n th\u00fac \u0111\u1ea9y ng\u01b0\u1eddi ta t\u00ecm \u0111\u1ebfn m\u1ed9t l\u1ed1i s\u1ed1ng b\u1ec1n v\u1eefng h\u01a1n, \u00edt l\u1ec7 thu\u1ed9c v\u1eadt ch\u1ea5t h\u01a1n.\n\nNh\u1eefng t\u00edn \u0111\u1ed3 c\u1ee7a ch\u1ee7 ngh\u0129a n\u00e0y c\u00f3 r\u1ea5t nhi\u1ec1u b\u1eadc v\u0129 nh\u00e2n, thi\u00ean t\u00e0i, t\u1ef7 ph\u00fa,\u2026 M\u00ecnh xin v\u00ed d\u1ee5 cho c\u00e1c b\u1ea1n v\u1ec1 Steve Jobs - v\u1ecb c\u1ed1 CEO \u0111\u00e1ng k\u00ednh c\u1ee7a Apple.\n\nSteve Jobs, ng\u01b0\u1eddi s\u00e1ng l\u1eadp Apple, l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t ng\u01b0\u1eddi theo ch\u1ee7 ngh\u0129a t\u1ed1i gi\u1ea3n. \u00d4ng tin r\u1eb1ng cu\u1ed9c s\u1ed1ng h\u1ea1nh ph\u00fac v\u00e0 th\u00e0nh c\u00f4ng \u0111\u1ebfn t\u1eeb s\u1ef1 \u0111\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n v\u00e0 t\u1eadp trung v\u00e0o nh\u1eefng \u0111i\u1ec1u quan tr\u1ecdng nh\u1ea5t.\n\nL\u1ed1i s\u1ed1ng t\u1ed1i gi\u1ea3n c\u1ee7a Steve Jobs th\u1ec3 hi\u1ec7n r\u00f5 trong c\u00e1ch \u00f4ng s\u1ed1ng, l\u00e0m vi\u1ec7c v\u00e0 thi\u1ebft k\u1ebf s\u1ea3n ph\u1ea9m. \u00d4ng s\u1ed1ng trong m\u1ed9t c\u0103n h\u1ed9 nh\u1ecf v\u1edbi r\u1ea5t \u00edt \u0111\u1ed3 \u0111\u1ea1c. \u00d4ng \u0103n m\u1eb7c \u0111\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n (ch\u1eafc nhi\u1ec1u b\u1ea1n v\u1eabn nh\u1edb nh\u1eefng bu\u1ed5i gi\u1edbi thi\u1ec7u d\u00f2ng s\u1ea3n ph\u1ea9m m\u1edbi h\u00e0ng n\u0103m tr\u01b0\u1edbc \u0111\u00e2y c\u1ee7a Apple, \u00f4ng lu\u00f4n xu\u1ea5t hi\u1ec7n trung th\u00e0nh v\u1edbi b\u1ed9 trang ph\u1ee5c gi\u1ea3n d\u1ecb, \u00e1o thun \u0111en vs qu\u1ea7n jean xanh) v\u00e0 ch\u1ec9 s\u1edf h\u1eefu nh\u1eefng m\u00f3n \u0111\u1ed3 c\u1ea7n thi\u1ebft cho c\u00f4ng vi\u1ec7c v\u00e0 cu\u1ed9c s\u1ed1ng.\n\nTrong c\u00f4ng vi\u1ec7c, Steve Jobs lu\u00f4n c\u1ed1 g\u1eafng t\u1ea1o ra nh\u1eefng s\u1ea3n ph\u1ea9m \u0111\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n v\u00e0 tinh t\u1ebf. \u00d4ng tin r\u1eb1ng s\u1ef1 \u0111\u01a1n gi\u1ea3n l\u00e0 ch\u00eca kh\u00f3a cho s\u1ef1 th\u00e0nh c\u00f4ng.
